          <h3 class="heading event-card__title">
      <a href="/events/star-clinic-super-parenting" class="heading__link">
      

<span>STAR Clinic - Super Parenting </span>

    </a>
  </h3>
    
          <p class="event-card__meta">
        The UCLA Family Stress, Trauma, and Resilience (STAR Clinic) is pleased to offer: Super-Parenting.
      </p>
    
    <div class="event-card__date">
                    

<div class="date-badge">
  <time class="date-badge__month" datetime="Feb">Feb</time>
  <time class="date-badge__day" datetime="27">27</time>
</div>
      
      <div class="event-card__date--long">
        
        <div class="event-card__date--wrapper">
